# Exercise 1 - Create a user profile property
<p class="block_">In this first exercise you will create a new custom property that can be accessed by the user in their profile and then defined by selecting and adding data.</p>
<p class="block_">Ignore steps 1 – 3 if you are already logged in as Steve in the SharePoint Admin center.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open Edge or the browser of your choice<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Browse to portal.office.com and login to your tenant as Steve<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open the Admin center and then open the SharePoint admin page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Click on <b class="calibre10">More features</b> then open the <b class="calibre10">User profiles </b>admin page<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre516" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-599.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_194"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="5">Click on <b class="calibre10">Manage User Properties</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre517" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-600.png"/></p>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_4"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_4">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">This may take a while to open the first time.</i></p><p class="block_3"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_10"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="6">Click on <b class="calibre10">New Property<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, Word, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre518" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-601.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Use the following values to build the new property<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">RangerTeam</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Display Name = <b class="calibre10">Ranger Team</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Type = <b class="calibre10">string (Single Value)</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre519" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-602.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36" value="4">User Description = <b class="calibre10">Please add your current Ranger Team assignment here</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_195"> </p>

<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_70" value="5">Policy Settings = <b class="calibre10">Optional</b> and <b class="calibre10">Everyone</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre520" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-603.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="6">Edit Settings = Tick the box to <b class="calibre10">Allow users to edit values for this property</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Display Settings =Tick the boxes for <b class="calibre10">Show in the profile properties section of the user’s profile page</b> and <b class="calibre10">Show on the edit Details page</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre521" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-604.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36" value="8">Leave the rest of the properties as they are and click <b class="calibre10">OK </b>at the bottom of the page to create the property<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_196"> </p>

<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_70" value="9">Scroll down the profile property page and find the custom property section where you should see your new property</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre522" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-605.png"/></p>
<p class="block_99">It will take some time before the property has been updated on the profile page so continue with the next exercise</p>

# Exercise 2 - Create a custom property mapped to a term set
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create a new People Term in the term store to allow a mapped custom property to use terms from the new term set.</p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_197"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In the SharePoint Admin center, in the left navigation select <b class="calibre10">Content services </b>and open <b class="calibre10">Term store</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre523" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-606.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>The <img alt="Home outline" class="calibre524" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-607.png"/> <b class="calibre10">Taxonomy</b> section of the tree view will be selected, in the <i class="calibre13">Admins</i> section click <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> add Steve to the Term Store Administrators and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> at the bottom of the page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre525" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-608.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">On the left-hand Navigation, next to <i class="calibre13">People</i> click <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> (if not refresh your web browser), then choose <b class="calibre10">Add term set</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre526" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-609.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3"> Call the new term set ‘Ranger Location’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre527" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-610.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Expand the Ranger Team and select <b class="calibre10">Add term<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre528" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-611.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Create 4 terms</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">East Yorkshire</li>
<li class="block_35">West Yorkshire</li>
<li class="block_35">North Yorkshire</li>
<li class="block_35">South Yorkshire<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre529" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-612.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">Return to the user profile management page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Manage User Properties</b> page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">New Property</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Use the follow values to build the new property</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">RangerLocation</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Display Name = <b class="calibre10">Ranger Location</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Select <b class="calibre10">Configure a Term Set to be used for this property</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69">In the Term Set picker drop down select the <b class="calibre10">Ranger Location</b> term set<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre530" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-613.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="4">Description – <b class="calibre10">Which Yorkshire Region are you based at?</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Policy Setting = <b class="calibre10">Required</b> and <b class="calibre10">Everyone – User can override</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre531" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-614.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="6">Edit Settings = tick the box <b class="calibre10">Allow users to edit values for this property</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Display Settings = Tick the boxes for <b class="calibre10">Show in the profile properties section of the user’s profile page</b> and <b class="calibre10">Show on the Edit Details page</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre532" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-615.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="8">Search Settings = Tick the box for Alias</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre533" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-616.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="9">Click <b class="calibre10">OK</b> at the bottom of the page to create the custom property</li>
<li class="block_35">Check that the new property is listed in the Custom Properties section<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Icon  Description automatically generated" class="calibre534" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-617.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_88"> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_198"> </p>

<p class="block_100">It will take some time before the new property is available in the user’s profile page. In the next few steps, you will be shown a shortcut way to find them which works based on the current office 365 Delve options.<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">On your Office 365 home page click on Steve’s name at the top right and click <b class="calibre10">My Office profile</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">On the page click on the button for <b class="calibre10">Update profile</b> then expand <b class="calibre10">How can I add additional information? </b>and then click on the <b class="calibre10">here</b> to go to your classic profile<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre535" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-618.png"/></li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_4"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_4">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">This won’t be necessary once the new profile properties become available on the main profile page, it just takes time this helps speed the lab up.</i></p><p class="block_101"><br class="calibre407"/> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">On the Edit Details page click on the additional options dots and select <b class="calibre10">Custom Properties</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre536" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-619.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_199"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="13">You should have the two custom properties created, fill in the properties with the following information:<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Ranger Team = <b class="calibre10">Blue</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Ranger Location + select the ‘<b class="calibre10">North Yorkshire</b>’ metadata value</li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Save all and close</b> then click <b class="calibre10">OK</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre537" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-620.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">There will now be a delay before the new terms are available to be used due to the updates that take place in Office 365 and the timer jobs and crawl schedules.</p>
<table class="table_13">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_69"><p class="block_4">You will know everything has updated properly as the Additional information panel will appear on your normal profile page.</p><p class="block_3"> </p><p class="block_4">This profile information can now be used as part of an audience, a search query and metadata use in document library columns. It can take a while for new profile columns to be available for use in search queries so have a try with finding user search data in the search module.</p><p class="block_3"> </p></td>
<td class="td_70"><p class="block_4"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre538" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-621.png"/></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>

# Exercise 3 - Configure My Site cleanup
<p class="block_">In this final exercise you are going to configure a secondary manager to allow access to a user’s My Site if it is being deleted.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18"><span class="calibre97">To return to the user profile management page, in the left navigation of the SharePoint admin center, click on  </span><b class="calibre10">More features</b> then on the right, open <b class="calibre10">User profiles</b> <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Click on the<b class="calibre10"> Setup My Sites </b>link<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre539" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-622.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Scroll down the page and in the <i class="calibre13">My Site Cleanup</i> section add <b class="calibre10">Steve</b> as a Secondary Owner and check name<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre540" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-623.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="4">Click on<b class="calibre10"> OK</b> at the bottom of the page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_">You have now allowed Steve to access every deleted site that is tombstoned for 30 days before being purged</p>
<p class="block_">This concludes Lab C</p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_201"> </p>

<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre4" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image63.png"/></p>

# Lab D – Working with data connections
<p class="block_">SharePoint is the backbone of content in Office/Microsoft 365 and therefore has a high level of integration with the low code/no code developer stack, the Power Platform. In this lab we will explore the integration of SharePoint lists with Power Apps by building a custom mobile app, create a workflow with Power Automate and report on our data with Power BI.</p>

# Exercise 1 - Create a new Power Apps form
<p class="block_102">In this first exercise you want to create new ways for users to add data to a SharePoint list. So, you are going to create a new list, populate it with data and then from there create a Power Apps form to allow users to complete the form from mobile apps and SharePoint.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_103"><span class="text_22">Open your browser and open your sales subsite in SharePoint Online - </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales</a><span class="text_22"> replacing XXXX with your tenant number<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">In the left-hand navigation or via the cog click on <b class="calibre10">Site contents</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">+ New</b> drop down and select a List<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre541" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-624.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Use the <b class="calibre10">From Excel </b>option<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Choose <b class="calibre10">Upload file</b> and navigate to C:\Labs\LabD and select <b class="calibre10">Sales Commission Payments</b> then click <b class="calibre10">Open</b></li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Next </b>on the ‘Customize’ menu<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Call the list ‘Sales Commission Payments’ and click <b class="calibre10">Create</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre542" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-625.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">In the new list and click on the <b class="calibre10">+ Add column</b> option and select <b class="calibre10">Yes/No</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre543" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-626.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_204"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Name the column ‘Commission Approved’ and make the default set to <b class="calibre10">No</b> and <b class="calibre10">Save</b> the column<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre544" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-627.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Add another <b class="calibre10">Person</b> column called ‘Commission Stakeholder’ and <b class="calibre10">Save </b>the column<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre545" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-628.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_205"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="11">You should now have two extra columns in your list<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre546" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-629.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Next, we will need to add some extra data to this list, the easiest way to do this is to click on <b class="calibre10">Edit in grid view</b> in the ribbon<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre547" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image668.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In grid view, copy the data from the SAMPLE columns into the new Commission Approved and Commission Stakeholder columns <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre548" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-630.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_206"> </p>

<p class="block_55">This would be the end result (use keyboard shortcuts like <b class="calibre10">Ctrl C</b> and <b class="calibre10">Ctrl V</b> to copy and paste<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre549" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-631.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="14">In the ribbon click <b class="calibre10">Exit grid view</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Delete the <b class="calibre10">SAMPLE Approval </b>and <b class="calibre10">SAMPLE Stakeholder</b> columns by</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Clicking on the columns heading</li>
<li class="block_35">Select <b class="calibre10">Column settings</b></li>
<li class="block_35"><b class="calibre10">Edit</b></li>
<li class="block_35"><b class="calibre10">Delete</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Then delete again</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="16">To create a custom mobile app for this list, in the ribbon select <b class="calibre10">Integrate</b> followed by <b class="calibre10">Power Apps</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Create an app</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_81"> </p>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre550" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-632.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_207"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="17">In the Power Apps pop up give the new form a name of ‘Submit your commission’ and click <b class="calibre10">Create</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre551" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-633.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="18">Power Apps will now build your app, you may need to select your region when the studio opens, after you make a selection click <b class="calibre10">Get started</b></li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_4"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_4">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">If you select your region and get environment not found repeat step 13 and 14.</i></p><p class="block_3"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="19">After the app is created in the canvas builder, click on the <b class="calibre10">Preview the app</b> button in top right to test the app<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre552" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-634.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_208"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="20">In the form view click on the <b class="calibre10">+</b> sign to create a new item<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre553" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-635.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="21">In the field values use the following:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Title = <b class="calibre10">CK750050</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Amount = <b class="calibre10">2999.99</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Commission Approved = <b class="calibre10">Off</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Commission Stakeholder = <b class="calibre10">Steve Smith</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre554" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-636.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="22">Click on the submit item <img alt="Checkmark with solid fill" class="calibre480" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-637.png"/> <b class="calibre10">tick</b> at the top right of the app to create the item<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre555" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-638.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="23">Close the Power Apps design page (click <b class="calibre10">Leave</b> if prompted) and return to the Sales Commission Payment list in the Sales site (go to site contents in the cog if you have lost your list page)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Refresh the SharePoint list, you should now have an extra list entry that was the one you created in the Power Apps app with the title CK750050<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre556" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-639.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="25">You have now created a Power Apps form in a SharePoint list <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>We could make further changes to the apps functionality e.g. remove the attachments field from the new item form or change the values for Commission Approved from Off/On to Yes/No<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>We could even theme the app and add our logo, publish the changes, select the apps audience and share it with them<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_26" id="id_Toc110854117"><b class="calibre10">Optional</b> you could now download the Power Apps app on your mobile phone, sign in as Steve, select <b class="calibre10">App apps</b> and you should be able to create another item on your mobile<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre557" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-7.jpeg"/></li>
</ol>

# Exercise 2 - Create a new flow in Power Automate
<p class="block_">We have an app that when published, will allow our sales team to submit the commission compensation. In this exercise you are going to create a new workflow so that a stakeholder is automatically notified in Microsoft Teams each time an item is added to the list.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the Sales Commission Payments list and click on the drop-down arrow next to <b class="calibre10">Integrate</b> then click on <b class="calibre10">Power Automate</b> then <b class="calibre10">Create a flow</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre558" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-640.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">In the templates menu click on the template for <b class="calibre10">Send a customised email when a new SharePoint list item is added</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre559" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-641.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">A new tab will open, select your region and click <b class="calibre10">Get started</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Click <b class="calibre10">Accept</b> on the cookies banner at the bottom of the page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_209"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="5">You will arrive on a page with the title of the workflow template we selected, scroll down on the page and click <b class="calibre10">Sign</b> <b class="calibre10">in </b>next to any connector that is not signed in<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre560" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-642.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Create Flow</b> once you have green ticks next to the connectors<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">We get a pop up saying our flow is ready to go, we have decided to send our communications about the commissions through Microsoft Teams rather than as an email, click <b class="calibre10">Got it</b> and then on the flow management page, click <b class="calibre10">Edit </b>in the ribbon<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre561" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image684.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">In the flow designer, click on the title of the workflow at the top of the page, and change it to <b class="calibre10">Notify stakeholder of compensation in Teams</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre562" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-643.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_210"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Next on the last action titled ‘Send Email’ click on the <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> and choose <b class="calibre10">Delete</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre563" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-644.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">OK</b> to confirm<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">At the bottom of the canvas click <b class="calibre10">+ New step</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the search box type in ‘Teams post’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">From the selection of matching action, select <b class="calibre10">Post message in a chat or channel</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre564" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-645.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_211"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="14">Configure the action as follows:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Post as = <b class="calibre10">Flow bot</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Post in = <b class="calibre10">Chat with Flow bot</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Recipient – click into the recipient field to open the dynamic content menu, search for ‘Stakeholder’ and select the property <b class="calibre10">Commission Stakeholder Email</b> from the dynamic content pane<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre565" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-646.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Message: Create the following message using a mixture of static text and dynamic content:<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre566" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-647.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">At the bottom<span class="tab">      </span>or top of the canvas, click <b class="calibre10">Save</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once you see a green banner confirming the flow is ready to go, close the Power Automate browser tab<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre567" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image690.png"/></li>
<li class="block_23">In the Sales Commission Payments list use the <b class="calibre10">+New</b> button to create the following compensation request:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Title = <b class="calibre10">CK750050</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Compensation Amount = <b class="calibre10">5000.00</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Compensation Approved = <b class="calibre10">No</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Commission Stakeholder = <b class="calibre10">Steve</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Save</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre568" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-648.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="18">In the <b class="calibre10">app launcher</b> <img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre569" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-6.jpeg"/> position your mouse cursor over <b class="calibre10">Teams</b>, select the <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> and choose <b class="calibre10">Open in new tab</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">When asked, click <b class="calibre10">Use the web app instead</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">In the left menu in teams click on <b class="calibre10">Chat</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_212"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="21">Then select the <b class="calibre10">Power Automate </b>chat <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre570" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-649.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Review the message sent by the flow, note that the date format could be improved with a function, but we have a positive end result<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre571" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-650.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Close the browser tab displaying Microsoft Teams</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 3 – Analyse SharePoint data with Power BI
<p class="block_">Lastly in this lab we will explore the data in our list with Power BI. Power BI can create a more customised report with the help of the Power BI Desktop application. To keep the process of analytics concerning this list as simple as possible, we will explore the web UI accessible directly from SharePoint.</p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_213"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Within the Sales Commission Payments list, select <b class="calibre10">Integrate</b>, then <b class="calibre10">Power BI </b>and finally <b class="calibre10">Visualize this list</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre572" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-651.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">With our tenant you will have Power BI Pro as part of your E5 license, however you may need to sign in, to do so click <b class="calibre10">Have an account? Sign in</b> and sign in as Steve<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre573" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-652.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once signed in, repeat step 1 in the browser tab where your list is open, refreshing the page first (you can close the two Power BI tabs that opened)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">A generic report will be compiled<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre574" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-653.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">The visualisations in the report are automatically generated based on the data in the list, on the left of the report is a pane called ‘Your data’ which is showing you the columns from our list<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Each visual can be customised, position your mouse cursor over the visual titled, ‘Count of Commission by Title’ which is the orange clustered bar chart in the above image<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once your mouse cursor is positioned over the visual you will see a <b class="calibre10">Personalise this visual</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre575" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image697.png"/> icon, select it<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, PowerPoint  Description automatically generated" class="calibre576" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-654.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Change the following properties in the ‘Personalize’ menu</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Visualization type = <b class="calibre10">Donut chart </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre577" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image699.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Legend = <b class="calibre10">Commission Approval</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Values = <b class="calibre10">Compensation Amount</b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre578" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-655.png"/><b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Click on the <b class="calibre10">X </b>to close the menu, the visual should look like the one below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre579" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-656.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once your mouse cursor is positioned over the visual you will see a <b class="calibre10">Personalise this visual</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre575" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image697.png"/> icon, select it<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre580" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-657.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Change the following properties in the ‘Personalize’ menu</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Visualization type = <b class="calibre10">Funnel </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre577" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image703.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Category = <b class="calibre10">Title</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Values = <b class="calibre10">Compensation Amount</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Tooltip = add a tool tip and use the <b class="calibre10">Commission Stakeholder</b> field<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre581" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-658.png"/></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Click on the <b class="calibre10">X </b>to close the menu, the visual should look like the one below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre582" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-659.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>Note, placing your mouse cursor over a data point will display a tooltip, in step 11 we added the Commission Stakeholder to be displayed when the tooltips are shown<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Let’s try building a cost summary by customising the visualisation at the top right of the report using the <b class="calibre10">Personalise this visual</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre575" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image697.png"/> button<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre583" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-660.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Change the following properties in the ‘Personalize’ menu</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Visualization type = <b class="calibre10">Card </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre584" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image707.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Fields = <b class="calibre10">Sum of Compensation Amount<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre585" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-661.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">Click on the <b class="calibre10">X </b>to close the menu, the visual should look like the one below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre586" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-662.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">We will use a similar visual for the large bar chart on the right of the report, use the <b class="calibre10">Personalise this visual</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre575" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image697.png"/> button on the visual titled ‘Count of Sales Commission Payments by Title’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Change the following properties in the ‘Personalize’ menu</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Visualization type = <b class="calibre10">Multi-row card </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre587" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image710.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Fields = <b class="calibre10">Title</b> and <b class="calibre10">Compensation Amount<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre588" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-663.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="18">Click on the <b class="calibre10">X </b>to close the menu, the report should look like this<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre589" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-664.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="19">At the top left of the page select <b class="calibre10">Publish to the list</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre590" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-665.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_214"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="20">Name the report, ‘Compensation Analysis’ then click <b class="calibre10">Publish</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre591" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-666.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">What we experienced as a very basic editor, with a Power BI Pro licence a user can do more with the report, in the ribbon menu click <b class="calibre10">Edit</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre592" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-667.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Continue</b> <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">This editor is more comprehensive, you can resize and add more visuals to the report and even add more pages, third part visalisations and much more, try selecting a visual and resize it<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre593" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-668.png"/></li>
<li class="block_23">Make this visualisation half the width it was formerly as shown below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre594" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-669.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Copy and paste the selected card visual and position it next to the other card as shown below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre595" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-670.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Select the left card, then click on the <b class="calibre10">&lt;&lt;</b> button in ‘Filters’ pane to expand it<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre596" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-671.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Next, in the ‘Fields’ pane expand the table to see all the columns in the list<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre597" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-672.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Now, drag the field titled <b class="calibre10">Commission Stakeholder</b> from the ‘Fields’ pane into the ‘Filters’ pane for the ‘Filters on this visual’ section<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre598" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-673.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the filters pane, for the ‘Commission Stakeholder’ filter select <b class="calibre10">Steve Smith</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre599" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-674.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the ‘Visualizations’ pane right click on the field called <b class="calibre10">Sum of Compensation Amount</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Rename for this visual</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre600" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-675.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Rename it to <b class="calibre10">Steve’s Compensation Requests</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Next select the other card visual on the right and repeat step 28, and once the filter has been added, set the Commission Stakeholder to <b class="calibre10">Tom Gooch</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre601" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-676.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the ‘Visualizations’ pane right click on the field called <b class="calibre10">Sum of Compensation Amount</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Rename for this visual</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Rename it to <b class="calibre10">Tom’s Compensation Requests<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">There is more we could do here however the report meets our stakeholders needs for now, in the ribbon select <b class="calibre10">Publish to the list</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre602" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-677.png"/></li>
<li class="block_23">Close the Power BI web browser tab to return to the Sales Commission Payments list<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23"><b class="calibre10">Refresh</b> the web page and then in the ribbon select &gt; <b class="calibre10">Integrate &gt; Power BI &gt; Compensation Analysis</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre603" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-678.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="38">You will be shown the published report<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre604" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-679.png"/></li>

# Lab E – Managing the term store
<p class="block_">The term store enables an organisational taxonomy so that grouping and identifying content can be consistent across all site collections. In this lab we will set up the term store, creating individual terms and synonyms and deploy them using a content type. We will also explore delegated access for the term store.</p>

# Exercise 1 - Create a Term group and Term Sets
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create a new Term Group using the new content services UI and then add some term sets from a CSV file in your labs folder.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Log in to your Office 365 tenant as Steve and then open the SharePoint admin center<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Expand <b class="calibre10">Content services</b> in the left menu and click on <b class="calibre10">Term store</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre605" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-680.png"/><br class="calibre9"/>You may use the <img alt="Caret Up with solid fill" class="calibre606" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-681.png"/> arrow in the recommended message to collapse this area<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_218"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="3">Next to the term store taxonomy name click on the ellipses and select <b class="calibre10">Add term group</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre607" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-682.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">In the group name type ‘Retail’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on the ellipses next to the retail group drop down and select <b class="calibre10">Import term set</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre608" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-683.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_219"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="6">Click <b class="calibre10">Browse</b> and navigat to C:\labs\LabE and select the ‘ImportTermSet.csv’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre609" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-684.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Click <b class="calibre10">Open</b> and then select <b class="calibre10">Import<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">You should now have a Products term set with child terms<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre610" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-685.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_220"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Select the Retail Group Name and on the options select <b class="calibre10">Add term set<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre611" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-686.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">In the term set name enter ‘Locations’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre612" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-687.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11"> On the Locations term set open the options and select <b class="calibre10">Add term<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre503" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-688.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">In the term name enter ‘London’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Now add the following terms as well:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Leicester</li>
<li class="block_35">Bristol</li>
<li class="block_35">Newcastle</li>
<li class="block_67">Dublin<span class="calibre93" id="id_Toc110854120"><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre613" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-689.png"/></span></li>
</ol>

# Exercise 2 - Manage Terms with synonyms and pinning
<p class="block_">In this exercise you are going to add some additional term synonyms associated with an existing term and then pin an existing term to a different term set.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In the content services term store expand ‘Retail’ then ‘Products’ then expand ‘Clothing’ and highlight ‘Headwear’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre614" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-690.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Select English in the Language options and then click on edit on the ellipses<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre615" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-691.png"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">In the ‘Synonyms’ field enter the word ‘Hat’ then click on ‘add’ and create another new Synonym called ‘Headgear’.<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> on the bottom of the page to add the new synonyms, after crawl has caught up you will be able to search by any of these terms<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Application  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre616" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-692.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="5">On the term store select the taxonomy name at the top level<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre617" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-693.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_221"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="6">Create a new term group <b class="calibre10">Stores</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre618" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-694.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Select the new group and create a new term set called <b class="calibre10">Products<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre619" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-695.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">Expand Retail &gt; Products and highlight Clothing and select <b class="calibre10">Pin term</b> in the options<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre620" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-696.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Expand the <b class="calibre10">Stores</b> group, then select <b class="calibre10">Products<br class="calibre9"/></b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre621" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-697.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Pin</b> at the bottom of the page to commit the change<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Return to the terms store and expand the products term set under stores and you should now have the terms tree linked from the Retail term set<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Table  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre622" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-698.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">If you now add more terms to the retail – footwear term set, they will automatically show in the store’s products term set as the master is based on the retail / products / clothing term set.</p>

# Exercise 3 - Create a tenant wide content type
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create a new content type at the tenant level, add some metadata columns and publish it to be available across the organization.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In your content services section, click on Content Type Gallery<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre623" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-699.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="2">Click on <b class="calibre10">+ Create content type<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_22" id="calibre_pb_222"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="3">Configure it as follows:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">Core contract</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Category = select <b class="calibre10">Create a new category </b>and call it ‘<b class="calibre10">Contracts</b>’</li>
<li class="block_35">Parent category = <b class="calibre10">Document Content Types</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Content type = <b class="calibre10">Document</b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre624" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-700.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Click on <b class="calibre10">Create</b> and <span class="text_17">remain</span> on the content type properties page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open File explorer on your computer and navigate to your Documents folder<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Create a new word file called ‘Core contract’ by right clicking in you Document folder, select <b class="calibre10">New</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Microsoft Word document</b>, name it Core contract, open it and add some text to a header or footer or just add a table to make it a template</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre625" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-701.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="7">Return to the ‘Core contract’ content type tab in your browser<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_223"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">In the core contract content type click on <b class="calibre10">Settings</b> and then select <b class="calibre10">Advanced settings<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre626" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-702.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55">Select <b class="calibre10">Upload a new document template</b>, click on <b class="calibre10">Upload</b> and then select your new contract word document you just created in your documents folder then click <b class="calibre10">Open</b> to upload it<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre627" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-703.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Scroll down and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> to commit the new template<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the ‘Core contract’ properties scroll down and in the ‘Site columns’ section click on <br class="calibre9"/><b class="calibre10">+ Add site column</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre628" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-704.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_224"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="11">Select <b class="calibre10">Create new site column</b> and use the following parameters:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">Store Location</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Description = <b class="calibre10">Store location for contract information</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Category = ‘<b class="calibre10">Create a new category</b>’</li>
<li class="block_35">New category name = <b class="calibre10">Stores</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Type = <b class="calibre10">Managed metadata</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Select term set – Select <b class="calibre10">Retail</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Locations</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, diagram, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre629" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-705.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="7">Do not use a default value</li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> to add the column<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">In the core contract options click on <b class="calibre10">Publish</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre630" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-706.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_225"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="13">On the Manage Publishing page click on <b class="calibre10">Save</b> to commit the publishing<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57">The content type will now be added to a timer job to publish the content type out to all site collections. To complete this lab later as it will take up to 1 hour for the content type to appear you can follow these steps to use the content type:<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_96" id="id_Toc110854122">Create a new document library<i class="calibre13"> </i>in Sales subsite called Contracts SS, click <b class="calibre10">+New</b> and name the library <b class="calibre10">Contracts SS </b>and select <b class="calibre10">Create</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_105"> </p>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre631" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-707.png"/></p>
<p class="block_105"> </p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_31" value="2">Click <b class="calibre10">+ Add column</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Add a content type </b>and click <b class="calibre10">Next<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre632" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-708.png"/><b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_31">In ‘Choose content type’ select <b class="calibre10">Core contract</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Apply</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre633" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-709.png"/><b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_97">Return to the document library and you should now be able to create a new document using the Core contract template instead of the default blank document. Select <b class="calibre10">+New</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Core Contract<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre634" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-710.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_106"> </p>
