# Exercise 4 - Configure delegated administration
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will set different administrators to manage the term store and the groups you have just created.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_84">In the <b class="calibre10">Term store</b> management page select the <b class="calibre10">Taxonomy</b> name<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_226"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="2">In the Admins section click <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> and add ‘Pete’ and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> on the page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre635" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-711.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_95" value="3"><span class="text_22">Open the cktraining SharePoint site collection home page - </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining</a><span class="text_23"><br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_23">In the <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> select <b class="calibre10">Site permissions</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre511" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-712.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Click on <b class="calibre10">Add members</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Add members to group</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Add members</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Select Pete and click <b class="calibre10">Save<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Pete</b> drop down and make him an <b class="calibre10">Owner</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a phone  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre636" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-713.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_95" value="9"><span class="text_22">Sign out of Office 365 as Steve, close the browser<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>Open a new browser and sign in to portal.office.com as </span><a class="text_23" href="mailto:Pete@CKXXXX.onmicrosoft.com">Pete@CKXXXX.onmicrosoft.com</a><span class="text_22"> with a password of SpAdmin365. (replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_95"><span class="text_22">Open </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com</a><span class="text_23">/sites/cktraining</span><span class="text_22"> replacing XXXX with your tenant name (Pete should have access to this site)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_23">On the SharePoint <b class="calibre10">cog</b> click <b class="calibre10">Site information</b> – then <b class="calibre10">View all site settings<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">In the Site Administration section click on <b class="calibre10">Term store management</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre637" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-714.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55">You are now going to confirm that Pete has got the right delegated level of access to manage the term set and configure additional groups and permissions<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="13">On the taxonomy page create a new term group called ‘Media’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre638" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-715.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="14">Select the <b class="calibre10">Media</b> group and in the Group Managers section click <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> and add the following users:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Managers = <b class="calibre10">Shannen</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Contributors = <b class="calibre10">Ashley</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Save</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre639" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-716.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">Select the <b class="calibre10">Media </b>group and create a new Term set called ‘Assets’ by clicking the <b class="calibre10">ellipse</b>, <b class="calibre10">Add Term set</b> or you can select the <b class="calibre10">Media</b> group and select from the toolbar <b class="calibre10">Add term Set</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre640" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-717.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="16">Highlight the <b class="calibre10">Assets</b> Term set and in the <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> <b class="calibre10">properties</b> page, set the default owner to ‘Shannen’ and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre641" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-718.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre642" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-719.png"/></p>
<p class="block_16"><span class="text_9">You have now successfully delegated administration control to multiple users at multiple levels in the term store. </span><span class="text_24">This concludes Lab E.</span></p>
<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre4" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image63.png"/></p>

# Lab F – Configuring Search
<p class="block_">Search is a key tool for end users to quickly find content. Although search is great right out of the box, it can be customised based on an organisations needs. In this lab we will look at running a search query in the modern SharePoint search, searching hub sites and associated sites, creating search acronyms, bookmarks, locations and designing a Q&amp;A experience.</p>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_4"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_4">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">This lab does rely on previous labs to work. However, if you do not have the destinations used in this lab you can create them as part of the exercises.</i></p><p class="block_3"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_40"> </p>
<p class="block_20">IMPORTANT</p>
<p class="block_">Some of this lab requires that the search and intelligence is fully provisioned on your tenant which can take up to 3 days on a new trial tenant. If the tenant is not fully provisioned, you can return to some of the lab to complete it at a later time.</p>
<p class="block_">You can tell if your tenant is ready by checking the search and Intelligence admin page and clicking the configurations tab. You will see if the tenant is not yet provisioned for Microsoft search.</p>
<p class="block_"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre643" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-720.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">To ensure there are some immediate take away skills from this exercise we will start off with exercises that are achievable without Microsoft Search being provisioned. All remaining exercises will be listed as optional, and as mentioned earlier, can be completed at a later time.</p>
<p class="block_5" id="id_Toc110854124"> </p>

# Exercise 1 - Run a query in modern
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will run a query using metadata in modern search and then elevate it to an organisational search query.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_103"><span class="text_22">Login to Office 365 as Steve and open the sales site </span><a class="text_23" href="https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales</a><span class="text_22"> and replace XXXX with your tenant name<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_23">Open the Contracts document library<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the search box type ‘contract’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre644" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-721.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55">You should see the two documents listed in the results pop up<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="4">Press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b> to see the full search results page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_230"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="5">In the results pop up box click on the <b class="calibre10">Expand search to all items in this site</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre645" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-722.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55">Now that you are at the site level for results you also get the sites included that host the documents and from here you can elevate your search to the organizational level<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre646" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-723.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_231"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="6">Click on Organization in the navigation to do a top-level search<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre647" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-724.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55">Notice that you now get more options in the filter and content type<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre648" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-725.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="7">In the search box type the word ‘shoe’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b> – select files in the tabs<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre649" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image775.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_232"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">You should now get 2 results listed <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre650" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-726.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Now change the query to <b class="calibre10">contract AND shoe AND sales</b> and press <b class="calibre10">Enter<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre651" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image777.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_57">You should now get filtered to one result. Sometimes teaching users simple search query terms can make searching content and metadata a lot simpler for them. Plus, it works in both modern and classic. <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre652" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-727.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="id_Toc110854125"> </p>

# Exercise 2 - Search across associated hub sites
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create some new documents and then search for them across hub sites.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the Customer alpha site <b class="calibre10">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/CustomerAlpha</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Create a new document in the Documents library called ‘sales contract ford123’ and add the word ‘shoe’ into the document and close the document<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre653" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-728.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open the Marketing site at <b class="calibre10">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/Marketing</b> (Or click on Marketing on the top left nav, as it’s linked through a hub association)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Create a new document in the documents folder called ‘sales contract kia456’ and add the word ‘shoe’ into the document and close the document<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre122" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-729.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Wait a few minutes for the crawl to run (Can take up to 5 minutes)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Return to the Marketing home page and in the search bar type ‘contract’, note if you are told we couldn’t find any results on this site, refresh the search</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_89"> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_234"> </p>

<p class="block_55">Once the crawl has finished updating you will see two search results for the new documents only from the associated hub sites<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre654" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-730.png"/></p>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Click on <b class="calibre10">Organization</b> to expand the search beyond the hub sites, notice you now get many more results covering all sites<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57" id="id_Toc110854126"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre655" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-731.png"/></p>

# Exercise 3 – Create an audience targeted search web part
<p class="block_">In this exercise we will set up a highlighted content web part. These web parts can be customised with a search query to help promote specific content. In addition to this, web parts can also be audience targeted at specific Microsoft 365 groups, we will aim to show this web part to a more exclusive audience.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">Firstly, we will need to map a crawled property to a managed property, to do this navigate to the SharePoint admin center as Steve </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/>Note that site columns do not need to be mapped to managed properties, we only need to do this because the column we wish to reference is a library column<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">In the left navigation select <b class="calibre10">More features</b> and under Search click<b class="calibre10"> Open</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre656" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-732.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="10">Select <b class="calibre10">Manage Search Schema</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre657" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-733.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_235"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="11">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Crawled Properties</b> tab<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre658" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-734.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the Filter box, type ‘product’ into the Crawled properties field and click on the green <b class="calibre10">apply </b>button<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre659" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-735.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Select <b class="calibre10">ows_Producttype</b>, this is a column we created in our Contracts library in an earlier exercise, this is the crawled result<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre660" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-736.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">We now need to map this crawled property to a managed property that we can use in KQL query, click on the <b class="calibre10">Add a Mapping</b> button<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Application  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre661" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-737.png"/></li>
<li class="block_19">SharePoint has some generic managed properties that we can link our crawled properties to, you can use the <b class="calibre10">Next</b> arrow to scroll through and select <b class="calibre10">RefinableString00(Text)</b>, or you can use the search to make this easier by entering in <b class="calibre10">RefinableString</b> and selecting <b class="calibre10">Find</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre662" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-738.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>This menu can be tricky to work with as it has two scroll bars, use the outer scroll bar to get to the OK button</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="16">Ensure the property appears as shown below<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre663" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-739.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Scroll to the bottom of the page and click <b class="calibre10">OK</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55">We can now reference RefinableString00 in our KQL query, to use KQL query in a web part, open the marketing site collection home page as Steve <b class="calibre10">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/Marketing</b><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="18">On the home page of the Marketing site, click <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> at the top right edge of the page<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre511" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-740.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="19">Move your mouse cursor to the white area above the News web part, an add web part button will appear, click on the <b class="calibre10">(+)</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre664" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-741.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">In the web part menu, search for ‘highlighted content’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_236"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="21">Select the <b class="calibre10">Highlighted content</b> web part<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre665" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-742.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">At the top left of the web part, type in the title ‘Sales contracts’<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre666" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-743.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">With the web part selected, click on the <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> button in the menu<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre667" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-744.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Currently the web part is displaying all files in the hub, which includes the Marketing and the Customer Alpha sites, this can be customised further as a Filter or a Custom query<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_237"> </p>

<p class="block_55">The filter offers a more user friendly way to write queries allowing end users to select the scope and parameters of the filter without using code, however the Custom query although requiring either KQL or CAML queries to run can offer more options, select <b class="calibre10">Custom query</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre668" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-745.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="25">In the Source drop down select <b class="calibre10">All sites</b> to give us a larger scope of content to work with (presently we do not have a large amount of content in SharePoint)<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A picture containing background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre669" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-746.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the Query text (KQL) enter the following:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">filetype:docx RefinableString00:shoe <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="27">Click <b class="calibre10">Apply</b>, note that it will take time for the search crawl to pick up the assignment of our crawled properties association with the managed property, RefinableString00, therefore when you click <b class="calibre10">Apply</b> below the Query text, you’ll either see the correct results (bottom left) or the unsuccessful query (bottom right)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_7">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_56"><p class="block_82"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre670" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-747.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_57"><p class="block_82"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre671" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-748.png"/></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/>If your results are unsuccessful, do not worry, the query is correct and will work once the properties are crawled, for now continue with the exercise<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="28">In the Sort by drop down select <b class="calibre10">Most viewed</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_238"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="29">Next enable audience targeting<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre672" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-749.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the Layout options, select your preferred layout, we will use <b class="calibre10">Compact</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, table  Description automatically generated" class="calibre673" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-750.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">At the top of the page, in the ribbon click <b class="calibre10">Republish </b>and confirm by selecting <b class="calibre10">Republish</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">We have enabled audience targeting in the web part, this means that we can configure the library so that the files only appear to specific audiences, to do this, navigate to <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><b class="calibre10">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales/</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Select the ‘Contracts’ library<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_239"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="34">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> and then choose <b class="calibre10">Library settings</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre674" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-751.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23"><span class="calibre97">In Library settings select  </span><b class="calibre10">More library settings<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre675" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-752.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="36">Under the heading ‘General Settings’ select <b class="calibre10">Audience targeting settings</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre676" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-753.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Select <b class="calibre10">Enable audience targeting</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre677" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-754.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Then at the bottom of the page, click <b class="calibre10">OK</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the breadcrumb trail at the top of the page click on <b class="calibre10">Contracts</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre678" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-755.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the Contracts library, ‘right click’ on the document titled <b class="calibre10">Contract alpha financials</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Details</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_31">In the details pane, scroll down and click on the ‘Audience’ field and enter <b class="calibre10">Marketing</b> and then select <b class="calibre10">Marketing Memvers</b>, when looking at a web part utilising audience targeting, like our highlighted content webpart on the marketing page, only people in this group will see the file (you can add up to 10 security groups)<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre679" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-756.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_31">Click away from the field to apply the property, then with the details pane still open, remove the tick from the Contract alpha financials document, then place a tick next to the <b class="calibre10">Sales contract alpha</b> document<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre680" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-757.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_31">With the Sales contract alpha document selected, the details pain will show the properties for this file, this time scroll down to the ‘Audience’ field and enter <b class="calibre10">Team CK </b>and select <b class="calibre10">Team CK Members</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre681" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-758.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_31">Click away from the field to apply the property then close the details pane, we have now configured these files to display to different audiences when viewed through a webpart that has audience targeting enabled </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_107"><br class="calibre9"/> </p>

# Exercise 4 - [Optional] Create a new acronym
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create a new acronym and point to a site location that will contain the specific data</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the marketing site collection home page as Steve <b class="calibre10">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/Marketing<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Create a new document in the <b class="calibre10">Documents</b> library called ‘ROI Opportunities’ and in the document type some text including ‘return of investment’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre682" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-759.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3"> Open the tenant administration home page and then expand<b class="calibre10"> All admin centers</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre683" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-760.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_240"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="4">In the list of admin centers click on <b class="calibre10">Search &amp; intelligence</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre684" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-761.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Answers</b> tab and select <b class="calibre10">Acronyms</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Add an acronym</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre685" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-762.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Create a new acronym using the following values:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Acronym Name – <b class="calibre10">ROI</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Stands for – <b class="calibre10">return of investment</b></li>
<li class="block_98"><span class="text_22">Source - </span><a class="text_23" href="https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/marketing">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/marketing</a></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre686" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-763.png"/></p>
<p class="block_108"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="8">Click <b class="calibre10">Publish</b> at the bottom of your acronym pane, then click <b class="calibre10">Close</b></li>
</ol>

<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_4"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_4">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">If you get an error trying to create an acronym check the search &amp; intelligence configuration – If the Microsoft search is not yet provisioned you may need to wait until the next day to complete this lab. You can however save it to Draft for now.</i></p><p class="block_3"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>

# Exercise 5 - [Optional] Create a new bookmark
<p class="block_">You will now create a new bookmark for a new company training portal link.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In the search and intelligence page click on the <b class="calibre10">Answers</b> tab and then select <b class="calibre10">Bookmarks</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Click on <b class="calibre10">Add bookmark</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre688" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-765.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Use the following values for your bookmark:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Title = <b class="calibre10">Company Training portal</b></li>
<li class="block_98"><span class="text_22">URL = </span><a class="text_28" href="https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining</a></li>
<li class="block_35">Description = <b class="calibre10">CK Training page for Office 365 Training</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Keywords = <b class="calibre10">Company training portal, skills, learning</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Categories = <b class="calibre10">training</b>, <b class="calibre10">skills</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Scroll down and click <b class="calibre10">Publish</b> <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">To publish a new Bookmark the search and intelligence must be provisioned so if service is not yet provisioned and you get an error try this part of the exercise later in the day or the following day.</i></p><p class="block_110"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Ensure your bookmark is listed<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre689" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-766.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">Open the marketing site<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the search bar type – ‘company training portal’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">You will get no results.<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">Click on<b class="calibre10"> Search the whole organization for company training portal<br class="calibre9"/></b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre690" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-767.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">You should now get a bookmark link for the CK Training bookmark<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre691" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-768.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55">If the link does not show up wait a few minutes and try again, publishing bookmarks are fairly quick to appear in search results<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">Click on the bookmark link which should open the CK Training site<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre692" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-769.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_26" value="11"><br class="calibre22" id="calibre_pb_241"/>
</li>
</ol>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_26" value="11">
</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 6 – [Optional] Create a location
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will create a new location based on your current office.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In the search and intelligence page click on <b class="calibre10">Locations</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Add location</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre693" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-770.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Use the following values for your location</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">Company HQ</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Country or region = <b class="calibre10">choose your country</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Address – <b class="calibre10">type your HQ address</b></li>
<li class="block_36">Keyword = <b class="calibre10">HQ, company headquarters</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_242"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="4">Click <b class="calibre10">Publish</b> when complete<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre694" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-771.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open the marketing site<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the search bar type HQ (Notice the local search returns no results again)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Click on <b class="calibre10">Search the whole organization</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_243"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">You should now get the HQ returned as a search result for all sites<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre695" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-772.png"/></p>

# Exercise 7 – [Optional] Create a Q&amp;A
<p class="block_">In this final exercise you will create a new Q&amp;A entry for a question query in search.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the search and intelligence page and click on <b class="calibre10">Answers</b> and then select <b class="calibre10">Q&amp;A<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Click on <b class="calibre10">Add question</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre696" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-773.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Use the following values for the new Q&amp;A</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Title = <b class="calibre10">Where is the marketing department</b></li>
<li class="block_98"><span class="text_22">URL = </span><a class="text_28" href="https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/Marketing">https://ckXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/Marketing</a></li>
<li class="block_35">Description = <b class="calibre10">This is the marketing department site</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Keywords =<b class="calibre10">marketing, department</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Click <b class="calibre10">Publish</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre697" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-774.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open the CKTraining site<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the search bar type the question ‘where is the marketing department’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Expend the <b class="calibre10">Search to the whole organization</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_244"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">You should get the site listed in the results (It may take a couple of minutes to show up)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre698" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-775.png"/></p>
<p class="block_40"> </p>
<p class="block_">This concludes lab F</p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_245"> </p>

<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre4" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image63.png"/></p>
<p class="block_10"> </p>

# Lab G – Configuring Apps
<p class="block_">SharePoint hosts a range of services, and where limits are reached, third parties often extend a helping hand in the form of an app. Traditionally in on-premises SharePoint deployments, organisations could install integrated applications to bring new capabilities to SharePoint like governance, automation and other enhancements. In the cloud, this is achieved by either acquiring apps from the app store or installing an app file. Once installed, end users can leverage these apps and admins can track their use.</p>

# Exercise 1 - Add a 365 store app
<p class="block_">In this exercise, you will log into Office 365 and add an App direct from the store.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Login to your tenant as Steve<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_95"><span class="text_22">Browse to the cktraining site collection </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com</a><span class="text_23">/sites/cktraining</span><span class="text_22"> (replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_23">In the <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> select <b class="calibre10">Add an app</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre699" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-776.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_248"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="4">In the My Apps page click on ‘From SharePoint Store’ then click on <b class="calibre10">Find more apps in SharePoint Store</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre700" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-777.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">In the search bar type ‘Support+’ and press <b class="calibre10">Enter</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre701" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-778.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">Click on <b class="calibre10">Support+ Help On-Demand </b>to open the information page for the app click on <b class="calibre10">Switch to the classic SharePoint Store</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre702" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-779.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_249"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="7">On the App home page click on <b class="calibre10">ADD IT</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre703" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-780.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">Click <b class="calibre10">Continue</b> and then <b class="calibre10">Purchase</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">After the App has installed click on <b class="calibre10">Return to site</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre704" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-781.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_250"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="10">When the trust App box pops up click on <b class="calibre10">Trust it<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre705" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-782.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11">Wait a few minutes for the app to install, you will currently be on the site contents page, refresh the page until the Support+ app is no longer greyed out<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre706" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-783.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">To test the app has installed correctly click on the <b class="calibre10">Documents</b> library <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre707" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-784.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_251"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="13">Click on the <b class="calibre10">ellipses (…)</b> and the click on <b class="calibre10">Support+</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre708" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-785.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="14">You will now be taken to the Support+ Trial home page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55">The App has been deployed successfully<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">You can click on the SharePoint navigation link on the top right to return to the training site when you are ready<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre709" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-786.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="id_Toc110854132"> </p>

# Exercise 2 - Add an app via the App Catalog
<p class="block_">In the next exercise, you will go to the App Catalog and then deploy an app to it which can be used in your team sites. </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Browse to the SharePoint Admin center<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Go to <b class="calibre10">More features</b> and then click <b class="calibre10">Open</b> under the ‘Apps’ category<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre710" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-787.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">If presented with a welcome dialog, please close it<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">On the ‘Manage apps’ page, select <b class="calibre10">Upload</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre711" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-788.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="5">Navigate to C:\Labs\LabG\GlobalToolBar and select <b class="calibre10">pto-365-sharepoint-toolbar.sppkg</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Open</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_89"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="6">Once uploaded a pane will open allowing you to deploy the app to all sites, or allow the site owner to add it to their site themselves, we will choose the latter and select <b class="calibre10">Only enable this app</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre712" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-789.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Click <b class="calibre10">Enable app </b>at the bottom of the pane<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Once the app is listed as enabled, click <b class="calibre10">Close</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre713" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-790.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_253"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Check that the GobalToolbar app is enabled on the ‘Manage apps’ page<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre706" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-791.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_95" value="10"><span class="text_22">Browse to your cktraining site collection </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com</a><span class="text_23">/sites/cktraining</span><span class="text_25"> </span><span class="text_22">(replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_23">Go to the page <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> and click on <b class="calibre10">Add an app</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">In the ‘Apps you can add’ section click on the <b class="calibre10">Add</b> under the ‘GlobalToolbar’ app <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre644" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-792.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_254"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="13">The app will be listed as ‘Added’ and a green banner will appear at the top of the page confirming the process was successful<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre714" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-793.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">At the top of the page click <b class="calibre10">Back to CKTraining</b> to return to the site<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Notice at the top of the page is a new custom global navigation bar<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre489" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-794.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="16">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Site contents</b> <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_89"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="17">In the site contents menu, you will see all the apps in your site including the GlobalToolbar, position your mouse cursor over the app to reveal an ellipsis (…)<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre715" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-795.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on the <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Remove</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In some cases, you will need to return to classic SharePoint to remove apps, click on <b class="calibre10">Return to classic SharePoint</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre716" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-796.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">In the classic site contents menu position your mouse cursor over the GlobalToolbar app to reveal an ellipsis (…)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_255"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="21">Click on the <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> and select <b class="calibre10">Remove<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre717" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-797.png"/><b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">When prompted by your web browser, click <b class="calibre10">OK</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">After about 15 seconds the app will disappear from the site, at the bottom left of the page, click <b class="calibre10">Exit classic experience</b> to return to modern SharePoint<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre718" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-798.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/>You have now successfully deployed an app to the app catalog and tested adding and removing the app from a site.</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_89"> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="id_Toc110854133"> </p>

# Exercise 3 - Add an Azure app
<p class="block_">In this exercise, you will need to use Azure AD authentication to install an App that is Azure hosted and add it to your app launcher.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In your Microsoft 365 admin center open <b class="calibre10">Azure Active Directory</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre719" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-799.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once the Azure Active Directory page opens, to add an enterprise application you can click <b class="calibre10">+Add</b> drop down and select <b class="calibre10">Enterprise applications</b> or you can scroll to the bottom of the page and in the Quick steps section select <b class="calibre10">Add Enterprise applications</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre720" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-800.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">In the gallery search box field type <b class="calibre10">Training</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre721" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-801.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Select <b class="calibre10">Training+ Learning On-Demand</b> and then click on <b class="calibre10">Sign up for Training+ Learning On-Demand</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre722" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-802.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">On the Azure AD Single Sign-On click ‘Authorise’ (sign in as Steve if prompted)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre262" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-803.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">On the Training Plus App page click on <b class="calibre10">Accept</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre723" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-804.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">You may get the following Permission requested prompt pop-up, select <b class="calibre10">Consent on behalf of your organisation</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Accept</b>.<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre724" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-805.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55">The app has now been added to your tenant and launches for Steve, the next step is to manage it in Azure AD and assign it to users<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">Return to the <b class="calibre10">Azure Active Directory</b> home page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">To assign it to users, we will create a new security group called training+, in your Azure Active Directory home page select <b class="calibre10">+Add</b> drop down and select <b class="calibre10">Group<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre725" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-806.png"/><b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></p>
<p class="block_55">or you can scroll to the bottom of the page and in the ‘Quick actions’ section select <b class="calibre10">Add group<br class="calibre9"/> </b></p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A picture containing diagram  Description automatically generated" class="calibre726" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-807.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="10">To create a new security group follow these steps:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_70">Group type = <b class="calibre10">Security</b><span class="calibre97"> </span></li>
<li class="block_35">Group name = <b class="calibre10">training+</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Membership type = <b class="calibre10">Assigned</b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre727" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-808.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Select <b class="calibre10">No owners selected<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre728" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-809.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">In ‘Add owners’ add Steve as an owner of the group, by searching and selecting <b class="calibre10">Steve</b> from the list and then clicking <b class="calibre10">Select<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre729" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-810.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">Now add Ashely as a member of the group, select <b class="calibre10">No members selected</b> link and search for Ashley from the list and select Ashley then click <b class="calibre10">Select</b></li>
<li class="block_36">Lastly click <b class="calibre10">Create</b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre730" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-811.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_81"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11">In Azure Active Directory click on <b class="calibre10">Applications</b> on the left hand-side and select <b class="calibre10">Enterprise applications</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre731" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-812.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Click on the TrainingPlus App to open its properties<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre732" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-813.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Self-service </b>and change the following settings:<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre733" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-814.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36">Allow users to request access to this application = <b class="calibre10">Yes</b></li>
<li class="block_70">To which group should assigned users be added click <b class="calibre10">Select Group</b> link, select <b class="calibre10">training+</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Select</b> </li>
<li class="block_36">Leave the rest as the defaults and <b class="calibre10">Save</b> the changes<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre734" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-815.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_257"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="14">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Properties </b>of the app and ensure that the app is ‘enabled for users to sign-in and it is visible to users<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre593" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-816.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">The App has now been assigned and authorised to your tenant, but it will take some time before it is available in your personal apps, continue this lab and come back to this after a while to complete<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55">To get the app listed on your app launcher you first need it to be shown on your list of apps (this can take up to 1 hour to appear)<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_95" value="16"><span class="text_22">Open your CKTraining site collection </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com</a><span class="text_23">/sites/cktraining</span><span class="text_22"> (replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
<li class="block_19">Click on the <img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre735" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-8.jpeg"/> <b class="calibre10">app launcher</b> and show <b class="calibre10">All apps</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_258"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="18">Scroll down to the bottom of the apps lists and you will eventually see your <b class="calibre10">TrainingPlus Learning On-Demand</b> app deployed listed under other apps <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<i class="calibre388"> It can take a while for the app to show up. To see the App a little sooner click on ‘Explore all your apps’ and you should find Training+ in the All apps section.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Icon  Description automatically generated" class="calibre736" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-817.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="19">Once the app has appeared on your main app launcher you can pin / unpin it to the quick launcher, click on the ellipsis to the right of the app and click on ‘Pin or unpin to Launcher’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre737" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-818.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="20">You App will now be listed in the main app launcher<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre738" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-819.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="21">You can now test the app by opening it and seeing some trial content. </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_111"><span class="text_22"><br class="calibre9"/>If you would like to trial the full 800+ end user training videos of Microsoft 365 for your business contact </span><a class="text_23" href="mailto:sales@combined-knowledge.com">sales@combined-knowledge.com</a><span class="text_22"> and a full free trial can be set up for you<br class="calibre9"/> </span></p>

# Exercise 4 - Monitor app usage
<p class="block_">In this exercise, you will see which tools can help you monitor app usage.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_103"><span class="text_22">Open your cktraining site collection as Steve </span><a class="text_23" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com</a><span class="text_23">/sites/cktraining</span><span class="text_22"> (replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </span></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Cog</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Site information</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">View all site settings</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In ‘Site Collection Administration’ click on<b class="calibre10"> Storage Metrics</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre740" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-821.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Locate the Apps you have installed and that the SharePoint apps take up part of your storage quota but the Azure App does not<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Chart  Description automatically generated" class="calibre525" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-822.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Click on <b class="calibre10">Support+ </b>app to get more information and a breakdown of the app<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre741" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-823.png"/></p>

# Lab H – ECM
<p class="block_" id="id_Toc110854136">Enterprise Content Management is a means to deliver consistent experiences across multiple site collections. This deliverance can be quite broad and can include governance through labelling and retention, to records management. In this lab we will cover this spectrum including retention, eDiscovery, data loss prevention, in place records and records centers. Note that the last two topics are optional and could be covered in your own time.</p>
