# Exercise 1 - Create a Retention Label
<p class="block_">In this first exercise you will create a new retention label that also has classifiers and a record declaration action. To create labels, you must have the AIP feature enabled on your tenant. If you are using an E5 trial / tenant, then you will already have this feature. If you are using an E3 tenant, you will first need to add the AIP Plan to your tenant and users.</p>
<p class="block_">Although you will create the label now it will not be possible to use / see the label immediately after publishing it as it will take several hours before it is published and available in SharePoint. Therefore, after finishing this exercise, you can return to SharePoint and the label will be available to use.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Expand Admin center and open the <b class="calibre10">Compliance</b> admin center<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre742" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-824.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">In the compliance admin page in the left menu, scroll down and open <b class="calibre10">Records Management</b> and select the <b class="calibre10">File plan</b> tab<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre300" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-825.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Click on<b class="calibre10"> + Create a label</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Use the following values for your label:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">10 Year Contract</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Description for users = <b class="calibre10">Retain a contract for 10 years from the date it was last modified</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Description for admins = <b class="calibre10">Retain a contract for 10 years from the date it was last modified</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
<li class="block_35">File Plan Descriptors:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_5">
<li class="block_63">Reference ID= <b class="calibre10">CK Contract</b></li>
<li class="block_63">Business function = click <b class="calibre10">Choose</b><span class="calibre97"> and select  </span><b class="calibre10">legal</b></li>
<li class="block_63">Category = click <b class="calibre10">Choose</b><span class="calibre97"> and select  </span><b class="calibre10">compliance</b></li>
<li class="block_63">Authority type = click <b class="calibre10">Choose</b><span class="calibre97"> and select  </span><b class="calibre10">Legal</b></li>
<li class="block_63">Provision/citation = click <b class="calibre10">Choose</b><span class="calibre97"> and select  </span><b class="calibre10">Sarbanes-Oxley<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_94"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre743" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-826.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Select <b class="calibre10">Retain items forever or for a specific period </b>and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A picture containing graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre744" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-827.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Use the following values for the retention settings:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Retain for <b class="calibre10">10 years</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Retain based on <b class="calibre10">When items were last modified</b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="8">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36"><b class="calibre10">Retain items even if users delete<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre745" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-828.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_22" id="calibre_pb_262"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35"><b class="calibre10">Delete items automatically</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre746" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-829.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">Click <b class="calibre10">Next<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_19">Click on<b class="calibre10"> Create label<br class="calibre9"/></b><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre747" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-830.png"/></li>
</ol>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="12">After a short time, the publish options appears, Leave the setting as <b class="calibre10">Publish this label to Microsoft 365 locations</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Done<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre748" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-831.png"/></p>

<p class="block_56"> </p>

</ol>

</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A picture containing text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre750" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-833.png"/></p>

# Exercise 2 - Create an eDiscovery case
<p class="block_">In this exercise, you will use the compliance center to grant access to Steve as an eDiscovery Manager, build a new case and discover specific data stored in the SharePoint environment. Note however that for this lab to work you must have added the credit card data as per lab B. Adding it now will require you to wait some time whilst search crawls the new documents.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_84">Open your 365 Admin Center<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_266"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="2">Open the <b class="calibre10">Compliance</b> Admin center<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated" class="calibre756" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-839.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Permissions</b> in the left menu, and then under ‘Microsoft Purview solutions’ click <b class="calibre10">Roles</b> to open the role management page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre757" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-840.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Select the<b class="calibre10"> eDiscovery Manager group</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">If you have issues seeing the permissions option try a different browser InPrivate/Incognito mode or refresh the admin page</i></p><p class="block_110"> </p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Scroll down the manager page and click on <b class="calibre10">Edit</b> for eDiscovery manager <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated" class="calibre758" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-841.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="6">To choose the eDiscovery Manager select <b class="calibre10">Choose users</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre759" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-842.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_267"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="7">Then select Steve from the list and then click <b class="calibre10">Select</b><span class="calibre97"> </span><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre760" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-843.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Next<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre761" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-844.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b> to Manage eDiscovery Administrator <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Click <b class="calibre10">Save<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_268"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="11">Click <b class="calibre10">Done</b> <br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre230" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-845.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Close the role page and then Sign out of Office 365 and then sign in again as Steve to ensure you have the new permissions<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open Microsoft 365 Administration again and open the <b class="calibre10">Compliance</b> admin center<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">You have to sign out and back in so that the new permissions that you have assigned Steve in the eDiscovery manager role is updated to his credentials. If you still cannot see the options to manage the eDiscovery case wait a few minutes and try again and ensure when you sign out that you close all windows and the browser, then open it again to refresh the credentials.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_81"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="14">Expand<b class="calibre10"> eDiscovery</b> on the compliance page then click on <b class="calibre10">Standard</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre762" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-846.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="15">On the eDiscovery page click on <b class="calibre10">+ Create a case</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre763" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-847.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="16">Use the following values for the new case:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Case Name = <b class="calibre10">Financials Discovery</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Click <b class="calibre10">Save<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre764" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-848.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_269"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="17">In the menu click select the <b class="calibre10">Financials Discovery</b> case to open the case<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre765" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-849.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="18">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Hold</b> tab and then click on the <b class="calibre10">+ Create</b> button to create a new hold query<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre766" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-850.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="19">Use the following values for the new hold:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_32">Name = <b class="calibre10">Alpha files from SharePoint</b> – click <b class="calibre10">Next<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre767" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-851.png"/></li>
<li class="block_112">Choose the locations, switch toggle to <b class="calibre10">On</b> for SharePoint Sites then click on <b class="calibre10">Choose sites</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre768" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-852.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_31" value="3">Select the <b class="calibre10">CKTraining </b>site and click <b class="calibre10">Done</b> to select that site <br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre769" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-853.png"/></li>
<li class="block_31">You should now have one site shown in the locations list.</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre399" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-854.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_31" value="5">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
<li class="block_31">For the query keep condition card builder selected and in the ‘Keywords’ box enter ‘alpha’ and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre770" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-855.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_31" value="7">Click <b class="calibre10">Submit</b> on the review page and then <b class="calibre10">Done</b>, when complete to close the new hold page</li>
<li class="block_31">Wait for 2 minutes and then open the hold properties again for ‘Alpha files from SharePoint’. You will notice that the Hold statistics has now updated and is showing at least 2 items (the total number will depend on how many documents you have created with the keyword alpha). The hold status will be pending until the timer job has finished with the hold jobs. You can also click on ‘update statistics’ to refresh the items found.<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_104"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre771" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-856.png"/></p>
<p class="block_105"> </p>

<td class="td_72"><p class="block_82">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">If you are waiting more than 5 minutes for the status to update continue to the next exercises and return later to see if the status has updated.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="20">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Searches</b> tab and then click on the <b class="calibre10">+ New search</b> button<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre772" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-857.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="21">Use the following values for the Search query configuration</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36">Name = <b class="calibre10">Alpha documents</b>, click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_22" id="calibre_pb_270"> </p>

<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_70" value="2">Locations – <b class="calibre10">Enable SharePoint</b> and then <b class="calibre10">Choose sites</b> and select the <b class="calibre10">CKTraining </b>and <b class="calibre10">CKTraining/sales</b> for the sites then click <b class="calibre10">Add<br class="calibre9"/></b><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre773" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-858.png"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre774" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-859.png"/></li>
<li class="block_35">On the bottom of the locations page deselect the option for ‘Add App Content for On-Premises Users’ then click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre775" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-860.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="4">In the ‘Keywords’ box type – alpha</li>

<p class="block_69"><img alt="Application  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre776" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-861.png"/></p>

<li class="block_36">Click <b class="calibre10">Submit</b> and then <b class="calibre10">Done</b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_113" value="7">Select the search query <b class="calibre10">Alpha documents</b><span class="calibre97">  (You may need to wait for the search to start / finish before proceeding). Once complete in the summary you will see how many items have been found across all your SharePoint sites. This number will vary depending on how many you created with alpha included.</span></li>
</ol>

</ol>

# Exercise 3 - Configure DLP
<p class="block_">In this final exercise, you will use a DLP policy to discover documents in your SharePoint sites that match a specific legal value and policy tips for new document uploads.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In Office 365 admin center open the <b class="calibre10">Compliance</b> admin page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">From the left menu, select <b class="calibre10">Data Loss prevention</b> section and click on <b class="calibre10">Policies</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre761" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-877.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Click on the <b class="calibre10">+ Create policy</b> button<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre791" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-878.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_272"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="4">Select the <b class="calibre10">Financial</b>, then select <b class="calibre10">U.K. Financial Data</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre792" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-879.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">In the Name enter – <b class="calibre10">UK Credit Card Fraud</b>, click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Leave the default location for ‘all locations’ and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the ‘Define policy settings’ leave the default option <b class="calibre10">Review and customize default settings from the template</b> selected and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre793" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-880.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_273"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">On the ‘Info to protect’ page deselect the ‘<b class="calibre10">Detect when this content is shared from Microsoft 365</b>’ and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre794" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-881.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">In the detection value change it to <b class="calibre10">2</b> from 10, and select<b class="calibre10"> Restrict Access or encrypt the content in Microsoft 365 locations</b> leave the rest of the settings on the default and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer screen  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre795" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-882.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">On the ‘Customize access and override settings’ page ensure the checkbox for <b class="calibre10">‘Restrict access or encrypt the content in Microsoft 365 locations’</b> is checked, then change the value<b class="calibre10"> </b>to<b class="calibre10"> Block everyone</b> and change the override option to<b class="calibre10"> ‘Require a business justification to override</b> then click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre796" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-883.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11">Select the <b class="calibre10">Turn it on right away</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer error message  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre797" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-884.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Click <b class="calibre10">Submit</b> and then <b class="calibre10">Done</b> when it has created<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Now create a new document called ‘<b class="calibre10">Sales Financial Data</b>’ in the <b class="calibre10">Contracts library</b> in the <b class="calibre10">Sales</b> site <a class="text_4" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/cktraining/sales</a> and copy the credit card data again that you used in Lab B or just do a web search for <b class="calibre10">Test Credit Card Account Numbers - PayPal </b>and next time search crawls the library you will get an email notifying you of the DLP breach (in a trial tenant like the one we are using on this course, this email will not be sent, however in a production tenant the email would resemble the image below)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55">You can edit the policy to also restrict access and /or block the item<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre798" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-885.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55">DLP rules take about 10 minutes to start working on documents in the SharePoint library after being created, check back after 10 minutes to see the impact in the sales contracts documents library where you will see red flag icons on each document that is in breach of a DLP policy<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre799" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-886.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_274"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="14">Return to the Compliance center open <b class="calibre10">Content search </b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on the <b class="calibre10">+ New search</b> to create a new search<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre800" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-887.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_275"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="16">Use the following properties for the search query</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Name = <b class="calibre10">Credit card discovery</b>, click <b class="calibre10">Next</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Locations = Select the toggle and switch on<b class="calibre10"> SharePoint sites</b>, and disable <b class="calibre10">Add App Content for On Premises Users</b> then click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre801" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-888.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="3">In the Define your search conditions (search Query box) select the Query language from ‘None’ to <b class="calibre10">English</b> and click <b class="calibre10">Add<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_35">SensitiveType:"Credit Card Number”</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre802" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-889.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_36" value="5">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b> and <b class="calibre10">Submit</b> then when the policy has been created click <b class="calibre10">Done</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_276"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="17">After the DLP Policy is created select the <b class="calibre10">Credit card discovery</b> policy after a couple of minutes (waiting for the search crawl to finish) to see the results summary</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Timeline  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre803" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-890.png"/></p>
<p class="block_55">You should now see under ‘status’ that there have been at least 2 items crawled</p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre804" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-891.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="18">On the top of the pane switch to the<b class="calibre10"> Search statistics</b> tab and then expand <b class="calibre10">Search content</b>, notice you have 2 items and 1 location<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="A picture containing application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre805" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-892.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_277"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="19">Expand <b class="calibre10">Condition report </b>to see the breakdown of condition by location type<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre656" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-893.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="20">Click on <b class="calibre10">Review sample</b> at the bottom of the page, notice your SharePoint items are listed (It may take 30 seconds to load this page)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre806" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-894.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="21">Click on one of the documents to open it and in the message box, click on <b class="calibre10">Download Original Item</b> to download the file<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Table  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre807" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-895.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="22">Open the item in the downloaded folder to show the word document has now been extracted from SharePoint Online<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_">This downloaded item could now be used as evidence or simply as an archive of breaches for reporting purposes, this concludes Lab H – the optional Exercises are only to be done if your instructor asks you to.</p>

# Exercise 4 – [Optional] Configure In-Place Records Management
<p class="block_">In this optional exercise, you will enable the ability to declare a document a record in a document library in a classic collaboration site.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Login to Office 365 as Steve and open the HR site collection - <a class="text_4" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/</a><span class="text_4">sites/HR</span> (replace the XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">On the HR page click on the<b class="calibre10"> Settings</b> cog, select <b class="calibre10">Site information </b>and click on <b class="calibre10">View all site settings<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">In the Site Collection Administration section, open <b class="calibre10">Site collection features</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre808" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-896.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23"><b class="calibre10">Activate</b> the ‘In Place Records Management’ feature<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Image" class="calibre809" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image950.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">Create a new document library called ‘<b class="calibre10">Project Beta</b>’ and open the document library<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the project beta library click on the <b class="calibre10">Settings</b> cog at the top right of the page and click on <b class="calibre10">Library settings </b>&gt; <b class="calibre10">More library settings</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message  Description automatically generated" class="calibre810" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-897.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Click on the <b class="calibre10">Record declaration settings </b>option in permissions and management<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre811" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-898.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_278"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="8">Select the<b class="calibre10"> Always allow the manual declaration of records </b>and click <b class="calibre10">OK</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">We are only doing this to showcase the capability in production it would be better to create a workflow to automate this process based on a trigger value.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_81"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre423" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-899.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Create a new document in the ‘Project Beta’ library called ‘<b class="calibre10">Final Contract</b>’ and add some text to the document and save it<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_57"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, chat or text message, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre812" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-900.png"/></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_279"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="10">Select the document and on the <b class="calibre10">ellipses</b> <b class="calibre10">(…)</b>, go to <b class="calibre10">More</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Compliance details</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre813" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-901.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11">On the compliance details page, scroll down and click on <b class="calibre10">Declare as an in place record</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre814" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-902.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Click <b class="calibre10">OK</b> on the lock down item message</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="13"><b class="calibre10">Close</b> the compliance details page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Refresh the document library page and notice that the document has now checked out and been locked<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre815" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-903.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_55">The item is now read only until it has been un-declared and checked back in.<br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<p class="block_57">These actions will be audited and can only be performed by administrators and auditor rights. The ability to delete a library is removed when it contains a record.</p>

# Exercise 5 – [Optional] Create a Records Center
<p class="block_">In this exercise, you will create a new records Center site collection, set up content organiser rules and a send to location and finally send a document from a collaboration site to the records center for long term legal storage.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_84">In the SharePoint admin center, navigate to <b class="calibre10">Active sites </b>as Steve<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_280"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="2">Click <b class="calibre10">+ Create</b> &gt; <b class="calibre10">Other options</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre816" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-904.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the ‘Choose a template’ drop down, click <b class="calibre10">More templates</b> (if prompted, click <b class="calibre10">Reload</b>)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Select the new tab in your web browser tiled <b class="calibre10">Create Site Collection</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_281"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="5">Use the following values for the new site collection</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Title = <b class="calibre10">Corp Records</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Web Site Address = <b class="calibre10">corprecords</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Template selection = <b class="calibre10">Enterprise</b> tab – <b class="calibre10">Records Center</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Time Zone = <b class="calibre10">your local time zone</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Administrator = <b class="calibre10">Steve Smith</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Storage Quota = <b class="calibre10">5GB</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Server Resource Quota = <b class="calibre10">0</b><br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre817" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-905.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">Click <b class="calibre10">OK</b> to create the site collection<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>

<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">

<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">Wait until it has been created before the next step. It should appear in Active sites once the page is refreshed.<br class="calibre407"/><br class="calibre407"/></i><img alt="Image" class="calibre818" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-906.png"/></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">In the SharePoint admin center go to <b class="calibre10">More features</b> and open the <b class="calibre10">Records management</b> page<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre819" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-907.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Use the following values to create a new ‘Send To’ connection</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Display Name = <b class="calibre10">Corp Records</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Send To URL = <b class="calibre10">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/corprecords/_vti_bin/Officialfile.asmx</b> (replace XXXX with your tenant number)</li>
<li class="block_35">Leave ‘<b class="calibre10">Allow Manual</b>’ and ‘<b class="calibre10">Send To action</b>’ ticked and with <b class="calibre10">Copy</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Add an explanation for the send action e.g. ‘<b class="calibre10">This is a corporate record</b>’</li>
<li class="block_35">Click<b class="calibre10"> Add Connection </b>(if you get an error you need to wait for the records center site to finish building then try again)<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre820" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-908.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_108"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="9">Ensure the new ‘Corp Records’ connection is shown in the ‘Send To Connections’ list<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="10">Open the Records Center site collection <a class="text_4" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/corprecords">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/corprecords</a><b class="calibre10"> </b>(replace XXXX with your tenant number)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>

# Lab I – Managing options for SharePoint Online
<p class="block_">In our last lab we will be exploring a range of options to manage OneDrive sync, storage capacity and retention, update the managed paths of new site collections and optionally configure Information Rights Management (IRM).</p>

>[+] Exercise List (Click to Open)
> 1. [Activating Your Software for Class](#activating-your-software-for-class)
> 1. [Lab B – Working with Site Collections](#lab-b-–-working-with-site-collections)
> 1. [Exercise 1 - Create a new Site Collection in the UI](#exercise-1---create-a-new-site-collection-in-the-ui)

# Exercise 1 - Configure OneDrive options
<p class="block_">In this first exercise, you need to configure retention, storage and sync options for OneDrive for your organization.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the SharePoint admin center as Steve <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click on <b class="calibre10">Settings</b> in the left navigation<b class="calibre10"><br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">In the list of settings open <b class="calibre10">OneDrive – Retention</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre840" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-929.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Change the retention days for deleted sites to <b class="calibre10">90 </b>days and click <b class="calibre10">Save</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre841" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-930.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="5">In the Settings page open <b class="calibre10">OneDrive – Storage limit</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre842" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-931.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="6">Change the default storage limit for all OneDrive users in the organization to <b class="calibre10">40 </b>GB <br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre843" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-932.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="7">Click <b class="calibre10">Save</b> to commit the change</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">Before doing a change which reduces size in production, ensure no users have storage larger than this or they will need to delete content first before being able to store new data.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="8">In the Settings page open <b class="calibre10">OneDrive – Sync</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_292"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">In the sync page Select the box for <b class="calibre10">Allow syncing only on computers joined to specific domains</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Enter (copy / paste) This domain Guid which is an example of an on premises Active Directory domain.</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_5">
<li class="block_63">b63b4f44-58b9-49cf-8911-b36e8575d5eb</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_114"><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre844" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-933.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="2">In the Sync page select <b class="calibre10">Block upload of specific file types</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_35">In the extensions box enter the following file types</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_5">
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">Exe</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">Mp3</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">Mp4</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">Mpg</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">AVI</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">FLV</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">SWF</b></li>
<li class="block_63"><b class="calibre10">WMV</b></li>
<li class="block_63">MOV<br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre845" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-934.png"/></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10"><b class="calibre10">Save</b> the settings<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_89"> </p>

# Exercise 2 - Define Site Collection options
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will change the default site collection managed path to use ‘teams’ rather than having sites as the normal managed path. A managed path appears in a site URL as a prefix before the site name.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">In the SharePoint admin page, select <b class="calibre10">Settings</b> and within setting page select <b class="calibre10">SharePoint - Site creation </b>section</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="A screenshot of a computer  Description automatically generated with medium confidence" class="calibre846" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-935.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">Make the following changes to the page:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Change the ‘Create team sites under’ from /sites/ to /<b class="calibre10">teams</b>/</li>
<li class="block_35">Change the default time zone to your <b class="calibre10">local time zone</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Change the default storage to <b class="calibre10">10GB</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_69"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre847" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-936.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="3">Click <b class="calibre10">Save<br class="calibre9"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">Click on the <img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre848" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.jpeg"/> <b class="calibre10">app launcher</b> position your mouse cursor over ‘<b class="calibre10">SharePoint</b>’ click on the <b class="calibre10">ellipsis (…)</b> and choose <b class="calibre10">Open in new tab</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">At the top left of the page click <b class="calibre10">+ Create site</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Choose <b class="calibre10">Team site</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Name the site ‘<b class="calibre10">Project Delta</b>’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Note that in the site address, the managed path is now ‘teams’<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, Word  Description automatically generated" class="calibre849" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-937.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre10">Next</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">Add Pete and Shannen as members then click <b class="calibre10">Finish</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="id_Toc110854144"> </p>

# Exercise 3 – [Optional] Enable IRM
<p class="block_">In this final exercise, you will enable and use IRM (Information Rights Management) on your tenant.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18">Open the SharePoint admin page and click on <b class="calibre10">Settings</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="2">At the bottom of the page click on ‘Go to the <b class="calibre10">classic settings page</b>’ link<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre850" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-938.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the Information Rights Management (IRM) section enable the button for <b class="calibre10">Use the IRM service specified in your configuration</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Image" class="calibre851" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image994.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="4">Click on <b class="calibre10">Refresh IRM Settings</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Scroll down and click <b class="calibre10">OK</b> at the bottom of the page<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Open your HR Site Collection at <a class="text_4" href="https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/hr">https://CKXXXX.sharepoint.com/sites/hr</a><b class="calibre10"> </b>(replace XXXX with your tenant URL)<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Create a new document library called ‘Restricted Files’<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_19">After being created open ‘library settings’ by clicking the <b class="calibre10">Settings </b>cog, select <b class="calibre10">Library settings</b> and select <b class="calibre10">More library settings</b> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_294"> </p>

<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_18" value="9">Click on the ‘<b class="calibre10">Information Rights Management</b>’ link in the ‘Permissions and Management’ section<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_12">
<tbody class="calibre1"><tr class="calibre2">
<td class="td_63"><p class="block_82"><img alt="psNote32" class="calibre14" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-9.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_64"><p class="block_109">NOTE:<b class="calibre96"> </b><i class="calibre388">This could take up to 60 minutes to appear due to IRM only just being activated.</i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre852" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-939.png"/><br class="calibre9"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="10">Enable the check box for ‘restrict permissions on this library on download’ use the following values for the names:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">Permission title = <b class="calibre10">Sales Policy</b></li>
<li class="block_35">Description = <b class="calibre10">Sales IRM Policy</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated with low confidence" class="calibre853" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-940.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="11">Click on <b class="calibre10">SHOW OPTIONS</b> and select the following options:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35">‘<b class="calibre10">Do Not allow users to upload documents that do not support IRM</b>’</li>
<li class="block_35">‘After download, document access rights will expire after these number of days’ = <b class="calibre10">30</b></li>
<li class="block_35">‘Users must verify their credentials using this interval (days) = <b class="calibre10">15</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre854" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-941.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_4">
<li class="block_35" value="4">Click <b class="calibre10">OK</b> to save the changes<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_23" value="12">Open the Word client and create a new document in your documents folder called <b class="calibre10">IRM test doc</b> and add some text to it<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Now upload the document to your restricted docs library<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the library select the document to see the preview pane, you will notice that the Word Online cannot open the document due to IRM<br class="calibre9"/><br class="calibre9"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, website  Description automatically generated" class="calibre855" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-942.png"/></li>
<li class="block_23">Download the document to your PC then open it, you will prompted to sign and then an IRM configuration box will appear shortly<br class="calibre9"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the document properties, you should see the IRM policy display, click on <b class="calibre10">View Permission</b><br class="calibre9"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_55"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre856" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image-943.png"/></p>
<p class="block_56"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_19" value="17">You have now successfully setup an IRM policy</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_"><span class="calibre97">This concludes Lab I.  </span></p>
<p class="block_5" id="calibre_pb_295"> </p>

<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre4" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55238/epub/images/image63.png"/></p>
